
1a1(tha): / 'dus pa rin po che'i rgyud dri ma med pa gzi brjid rab tu 'bar ba'i mdo las theg pa chen po yum gyi cho ga bzhugs so// // 
1b1(tha): g.yung drung lha'i skad du na/
2a1(tha): mu ye khri gsal da ra phyod/ gang zag mi yi skad du na/ bka' zab mo shes rab kyi
2a2(tha): pha rol tu phyin pa/ theg pa chen po yum gyi dkyil 'khor gyi don bstan pa'i mdo/ rnam pa
2a3(tha): thams cad mkhyen pa sprul pa'i sku la phyag 'tshal lo// de'i tshe de'i dus na/ ston pa rnam
2b1(tha): pa thams cad mkhyen pa sprul pa'i sku des 'gro ba sems can gyi don la dgongs nas/ mi mdzhed kyi 'jig rten lho 'dzam bu gling gi dmig/ seg kha bon gyi 'byung gnas/ stag / 
2b2(tha): gzig rgyal po'i yul/ gnas mchog dam pa 'ol mo glang chen gyi dbus/ rgyal s po brang ging brgyad kyi gnas su/ mdzad pa bcu gnyis kyi don mthar byin par mdzad pa'i / 
2b3(tha): dus su/ bstan pa rjes bzhag gi mdzad pa'i dus la bab ste/ de yang spyir sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rjes su bzhag pa'i bka' rab 'byams theg pa rgya mtsho la/ bsam gyis mai 
2b4(tha): khyab cing brjod kyis ma lang yang / sgoMs su sems can gyi blo dngos kyi gdul bya la rnam pa gsum ste/ sku gdung dang sku gzugs gsung rab gsum gyis/ bstan pa rnam gsum rjes 
2b5(tha): sdu bzag par mdzad de/ de yang sku gdung dang sku gzugs kyi bstan pa ni/ kun tu rgyas par l la zhing mtha' yas par mdzad // de'i thugs bcud 'gyur pa/ bde bar gzhegs pa'i 
2b6(tha): bka' lung gsung rab con gyi rgya mtsho la/ 'bum 'gyur bye ba rtsis las 'das kyang / mdo ru bsdus shing grangs kyis dbye ba la/ md 'bum gzungs gsum man ngag dang bzhi ru 
3a1(tha): gsungs te/ de yang rgyas pa 'brum du bsgrags pa las/ rgyud lung man ngag gsag ba'i 'brum la bsam gyis mi khyab cing brjod kyis ma lan zhing / 'don mchod rgyas pa / 
3a2(tha): phye grangs kyi don du mtha' yas par gsungs kyang / de'i nang nas kun gyi mchog tu gyur pa/ bka' rgya che ba theg pa chen po/ shes rab kyi ph rol tu phyin pa sum gyi 'bum zhes / 
3a3(tha): bya ba/ re rgyal lhun po' po brang / 'odi kyi lha re songs bmtsan gyi rtsi mo ra gtan la pab ste bshad par mdzad do// de nas bka' shes rab kyi pha rol tu pbyin pa de dag/ 'gro ba 
3a4(tha): sems can gyi don du zhal dro ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rab tu byin che bar gnas pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kun bkra shes pa dang bde legs chen pos yongs su khyab 
3a5(tha): par mdzad par dgongs nas/ gnas mtcshog dam pa 'ol mo glang chen gyi byang thub/ dg rgyas yon tan gyi gling zhes bya bar byen nas/ ro bo chen po bkra zhes dpal brtsigs kyi 
3a6(tha): mdun/ rgya mrtsaM bbra shis khyud mo'i glang / nags tshal m tog pun tshigs kyi gnasala/ grong kbyer chen po byan glang khyud kyi dbuns/ sku mkhar cing ba dgu tig ga nang na/ 
3b1(tha): bram ze'i rgyal po kun dga' bzang skyong zhes bya ba dang / tshogs sbyor rgyu'i yin bdag dang bcas te/ me tog mdzes pa'i gling la byin nas/ 'khor du gtogs pa'i gnhen rab g.yung / 
3b2(tha): dung sems dpa' rnams dang / steng gi lha dang / 'og gi klu dang / bar gyi ma dang / phyogs skyong ba bcu dang / rgyal po chen po bzhi dang / 'jig nyen gyi dpal mgon rnams dang / lha ma 
3b3(tha): dge ba la phyogs pa rnams 'dus te/ gsas khang chen po para gling chen zhes bya ba bzhengs su gsol nas/ de'i nang du bde bar gshegs pa'i sku gzugs mtha' yas pa dang / gsung 
3b4(tha): rab 'bum sde bka' rgyud dang / theg pa chen po yum gyi don gtan la hab pa rnams/ rin po che sna lnga'i glegs bam du shams nas bzhugs su gsol te/ dga' ston dang mchod 
3b5(tha): pa rgya chen por mdzad do// de nas de'i tshe de'i dus na/ 'khor du gtogs pa rnams kyis ston pa la/ bla na med pa'i mchod pa rgya chen po spul nas 'khor rnams kyi nang nas/ 
3b6(tha): gshen rab g.yung dung sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po tshangs pa gtsug pud kyis/ rgyan dang cha lugs mdzes par byas nas lha'i me tog man dha ra ba lag tu tshogs nas ston pa'i 
4a1(tha): y/ dngdu 'thod// dus btzogs thal mo sbyar bar brld de gsols/ rnam pa tsams cad bkhyen pa'i ston pa lags/ 'og men dga' ldan gnas mcshog dam pa nas
4a2(tha): 'gro ba'i don du ched bzhes sprul ba'i sku/ 'd gsal lha las ram par bbs nas su / 'dzam gling 'og kha 'al mo glang chen du/ rgyal po'i sras su sku bzhes 'gro ba'i don/ 
4a3(tha): mdzad pa bcu gnyis bkod pa rim par mdzad/ da lha'i skabs su rjes bzhag mdzad pa la/ sku gdung sku gzugs gsung rab glegs bam gsum/ phyi ru rgya che grangs mang bsam mi / 
4a4(tha): khyab/ bskod pa rnam dag bsam mtha' yas lags kyang / sgoMs su da lha'i dus dang gnas skabs 'dir/ dge rgyas yon tan tshogs pa'i gling chen du/ gzhal yas phun tshogs 
4a5(tha): prna gling chen bzhes/ bka' rgyud phun tshogs rgyas pa 'bum du gsungs/ mdzad pa shun tshigs rnam par rgyal ba ste/ phun tshigs rnam pa gsum gyi mdzad pa yis/ steng gi lha 
4a6(tha): dang 'og gi klu dang ni/ bar gyi ma la sogs pa'i 'gro ba rnams/ dang spro dang 'dren dang ba'i yi ga bde/ ngo mtshar yid 'ong dpal 'byor phun sum tshogs/ rnam dag bkod pa bsam 
4b1(tha): mtha' yas nas su / rgya che mtha' yas ngo mtshar che lags kyang / bstan pa rnam gsum rjes su bzhag pa la/ mnga' dbul zhal bsro'i rim par mdzad nas su / thang cig dge 
4b2(tha): ba'i las mtha' byung mod kyang / ypun du bkra shes mtha' ru byin che zhing / bstan pa rab tu gnas par mi 'gyur bas/ bde bar gshegs pa'i sku gdung gsung rab la/ ston pas 
4b3(tha): mnga' dbul zhal bsro'i dus la bab/ ces gsol to// de la ston pas bka' stsal pa/ zhus pa legs so tshangs pa gtsug pud gnhen/ khyed ni sngon nas sgrib byang tshogs 
4b4(tha): s+dzogs shing / da lha'i dus 'dir las 'phro'i stobs hugs kyis/ sangs rgyas bstan pa'i zhabs 'degs dag la gnas/ rgyal ba bdag dang tshe rabs las 'phro mthun/ da yang bdag gi 
4b5(tha): bstan pa ma s+dzogs bar/ ma 'ongs 'gro ba sems can 'dul don du/ rgyun thugs 'bras tsob 'gro ba'i don du 'gyur/ mngon gyur ldog gyur sdul pa ci yang stoen/ 'gro ba rang 
4b6(tha): mthun cha lugs thabs kyis mdzad/ thugs rje rgyun mi chad pas gzhan don skying / rang don phun sum tshogs pa dag ldan nas/ sems skyed ma bzhis gzhan don mtha' yas 
5a1(tha): skying / mthar ni rang gzhan don gnyis mngon grub cing / zung 'jug spyod pas don gnyis mthar byin te/ bdag dang bka' rol gcig tu bsdus pa ste/ 'gro don / 
5a2(tha): bsam mtha' yas pa 'grub par 'gyur/ da lha'i dus dang gnas skabs 'di dag la/ khyed ni bdag gi bstan pa'i bon la dbang / lhag par 'phan yul 'don mtshod rnam gnyis kyi/ 
5a3(tha): bstan pa se la ba'i gnyen po khyed yin pas/ bstan pa'i mnga' dbul zhal bsro'i rim pa rnams/ gsung drung spyod lam zab mo mchog 'dzin cing / byang chub sems ldan khyod 
5a4(tha): la gnyer du gtad/ dge ba'i las la cang tshod mthar dbyung zhing / brtson pa mthar bhyin 'grus pas myur du sgrubs/ skal ldan skyes bu dam pas gnyer bzhes shig/ ces bka' 
5a5(tha): stsal to// de la yang tshangs pa gtsug pud kyis gsol pa/ rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa yi/ cir yang sprul sku ston pa lags/ bstan pa'i mnga' dbul zhal bsro' ram
5a6(tha): bdag la gnyer du gtad nas su/ thams cad mkhyen pas bka' gnang bar/ phyi ra bon sgo cag rgyud kyis/ phyi sgos hun tsam byed lags kyang / sgos su gang la gang dgos kyis/ 
5b1(tha): rab tu gnas pa'i rim pa rnams/ zung tsam dbye gshags mi pbyed pas/ bde bar gshegs pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi/ s+dzas dang yo byad ma lus dang / mchod pa'i yo byad gyur pa rnams/ 
5b2(tha): bdag cag zhabs nas 'degs lags kyis/ bder gshegs mchod pa'i go rim gyi/ ji ltar 'tshal ba'i rim pa rnams/ thams cad mkhyen pas bka' gnang 'tshal/ zhes 
5b3(tha): gsol to// de la ston pas kyang bstan pa rnam gsum rjes su bzhag pa'i/ bde bar gshegs pa'i sku gdung sku gzugs gsung rab rnams/ zhal bsro ba bya ba dang / phyei rabs kyi gang
5b4(tha): zag rnams la 'gro bsdrang ba'i dpe dang thabs su bstan pa'i phyir du / bka' shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa theg pa chen po yum gyi dkyil 'khor gyi don bstan par dgongs nas 
5b5(tha): 'khor rnams la bka' stsal pa/ ghen rab gsung dung sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po tshangs pa gtsug pud/ gnan yang mnga' 'og tu gtogs pa'i ghen rab gsung drung 
5b6(tha): sems dpa' rnams/ spyir sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rjes su bzhag pa'i don rnam pa gsum ni sku gdung sku gzugs gsung rab glegs bam gsum yin te/ de dag 'gro ba sems 
6a1(tha): can gyi don du pun du bkra shis shing mtha' ru byin che bar bya ba dang / sems can rnams sgrib gnyis byang tshigs gnyis srdzogs par bya ba'i ched du phye rabs kyi gang zag 
6a2(tha): rnams la bstan pa bzhag pa dang / 'gro ba thar par drangs ba'i dpe dang thabs su bstan pa'i phyir na/ bde bar gshegs pa'i mchod sbyin dkyil 'khor gyi skor la don rnam pa bzhi ru 
6a3(tha): 'byung ste/ de yang kun dbyings rgyal ba'i dkyil 'khor dang / par phyin sum gyi dkyil 'khor dang / kun 'byung thabs kyi dkyil 'khor dang / yongs s+dzogs shes rab kyi dkyil 'khor dang 
6a4(tha): bzhi ru 'byung ste/ de dag rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor re re la yang yan lag gi dkyil 'khor mtha' yas par 'byung ste/ sems can rnams sgrib gnyis byang zhing tshogs gnyis s+dzogs pa'i 
6a5(tha): ched du bstan pa'o// de la d lha'i dus dang skabs la bab ste/ bstan pa'i mnga' dbul zhal bsro ba'i cho gni/ bka' shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa theg pa chen po rnam par dag 
6a6(tha): pa yum gyi dkyil 'khor 'byung zhing zhal dbye ste/ de la yang yan lag sum cu rtsa gnyis kyis gtan la dbab pa ni/ de yang sngon 'gro gzhi yi yan lag la/ don rnam pa bcus 
6b1(tha): gtan la dbab ste/ de yang tsig mar s+dzas bsag pa dang / gzhi gnas bslang ba dang / dkyil 'khor brtsig pa dang / chag chag gdab pa dang / dag tshangs bya ba dang / snyan gsan dbab 
6b2(tha): pa dang / chas gos 'thog pa dang / sta gon gyi ram gro bya ba dang / dkyil 'khor bri ba dang / rgyan s+dzas dgod pa dang bcu'o// gnyis pa dngos gzhi lam gyi yan lag la/ don rnam pa 
6b3(tha): bca drug gis gtan la dbab ste/ dkyil 'khor bsgom pa dang / gdan 'brul ba dang / spyan drang ba dang / dgyes pa bskyed pa dang / khrus gsol ba dang / mnga' dbul ba dang / zhal bsro 
6b4(tha): ba dang / phyag bgyi ba dang / bshag pa bya ba dang / mchod pa 'brul ba dang / sku bstod pa dang / mtshan spyir bsdu ba dang / 'phrin las btsol ba dang / bkra shes mchod pa dbul ba dang / 
6b5(tha): mchod byin gtang ba dang / thon lam gdab pa las sogs pa'o// gsum pa 'bras ba grub pa'i yan lag la drug ste/ sgo dbye ba dang / lha nal bstan pa dang / dbang bskur ba dang / 
6b6(tha): lha bskyod pa dang / gzhal yas bsdu ba dang / bkra shis gsol ba dang drug ste/ de ltar du yan lag sum cu rtsa gnyis kyi bka' stsal pa'o// de la thog mar s+dzas dang yo byed bsag 
7a1(tha): pa ni/ bde bar gshegs pa la mchod pa'i rdzas dang / rang bzhin mkho bthun gyi yo byad dang gnyis te/ tshig mar bde bar gshegs pa'i rdzas la/ bar me dang / me tog 
7a2(tha): dang / dre zham bdug sons dang / lha sdzas kyi dro nam dang / nal zas dang / re mcshog dang / rga ghang dang / sgra snyan dang / ril mo dang / pe kha dang / hin dang / glang bu dang / sgong dang / shing / 
7a3(tha): ha dang / rmang bya dang / dbal dar dang / rgyal mtshan dang / gdugs dang / rgyab yol dang / ba dan dang / lhab lhub dang / dar dpyang dang / phye ma dang / 'byur ma dang / cang shes kyi ha dang / dung 
7a4(tha): gi glang po dang / ma ho'i mdzo dang / 'dod 'jo' ba mo dang / ma rmongs pa'i lo tog dang / dkar gsum dang / ma ra gsum dang / mchod pa'i bye brag dpag tu med par bsag pa'o// 
7a5(tha): gnyis pa mkho mthun gyi s+dzas la/ dkyil 'khor gyi rgyan s+dzas dang / gnhen po' chas gis gnyis te/ theg mar dkyil 'khor gyi s+dzas la/ gnam lhags kyi 'dzor chen dang / 
7a6(tha): bse'i g.yag pa dang / dung gi bre ba dang / rin po che'i phrad stsal dang / pad zhun gyi thig thag dang / gser gyi thig 'dzir dang / g.su'i sar so dang / rin po che'i sa phag dang / gtsang / 
7b1(tha): ma'i chab lnga dang / sman songs me tog dang / sa tshen sna lnga dang / rin chen bum pa dang / ma 'dil rkang gsum dang / gnam rgyan dang / yol ba dang / bla bre dang / mda' dar dang / me / 
7b2(tha): long dang / ral byu dang / mchod pa'i bye brag la sogs pa'o// gnyis pa gnhin po' chas gos la/ dbu rgyan dang / snyan cha dang / mbgur chu dang / dpung rgyan dang / phyag gdub dang / 
7b3(tha): zhabs gdub dang / stod g.yogs dang / snad sham dang / sku chings dang / re shreng dang / gtsang gos dang / gtsang lham dang / gtsang thoMd dang / phyag rgya'i phu rlung dang / dar dkar gyi cig zhu la 
7b4(tha): sogs pa phun sum tshogs pa'i yo byad la/ ma tshang zhing ma tshogs pa med par bsag pa'o// de ltar du bde bar gshegs pa mchod pa'i yo byad la/ ma tshang ba dang ma tshigs pa med 
7b5(tha): par phun sum tshogs pa ru bsags pas/ bdag dang mtha' yas pa'i sems can rnams/ sgrib gnyis byang zhing tshogs gnyis s+dzogs nas/ myur du bla na med pa yang dag par s+dzogs 
7b6(tha): pa'i sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang 'thob par 'gyur ro// tshangs pa gtsug pud de'i phyir na/ bde bar gshegs pa yum gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga'i s+dzas dang yo byad ma lus pa tshogs par / 
8a1(tha): // sog cig/ ces bka' stsal nas/ tghangs pa gtsug pud las sogs phun sum tshogs pa'i 'khor rnams kyis s+dzas dang yo byad rnams tshogs par bsags so// de ni 
8a2(tha): thig mar srdzas dang yo byad bsags par bstan pa'o// de nas yang ston pas bde bar gshegs pa yum gyi dkyil 'khor las/ gzhi gnas bslang ba'i cho ga mdzad de/ mdun du rten po / 
8a3(tha): che' snod bzang du 'byu sna' bshes gtsang chab lnga dang / sman 'byu dang / me tog dang / rin po che bsrtsal nas dkar chab kyis bran te/ rin po che gter khyim gyi phyag rgya bcas 
8a4(tha): nas/ a ~M hU~M gis snod bcud thams cad 'dod yin gyi phung por byin gyis brlabs nas tshegs su bcad nas gsungs pa/ o 'jig rten gsum gyi mgon mdzad cing / 
8a5(tha): sangs rgyas bstan pa dag la gnas/ dkar po dge ba'i grogs mdzad pa/ snang srd yongs kyi dpal mgon po/ s bdag khyab pa dbang chen dang / sa yi lha mo brtan ma dang / sa 'dzin 
8a6(tha): lag pa chen po ste/ sar khams lo skor sme ba gling / sa bdag klu gnyan gtod kyi tshogs/ ro bo'i rtse dang rgya mtsho' gting / chu bo' gzhung dang 'grim lam srang / g.ya' yang 
8b1(tha): srdjengs dang nags tshal gseb/ gdags re dkar dang ri bs re nag/ dben gnas dag la gnas pa kun/ dng gi gtsang ma'i gnas 'dira/ mchod byin mkrin du spyan 'dren na// 
8b2(tha): 'khor bcas ma lus gshegs su gsol/ bdag gi ting 'dzin stobs dang ni/ de bzhin nyid kyi stobs kyis ni/ snang srid lha yi gzhal yas kun/ rin chen gter gyis gang bar 
8b3(tha): sprul/ mchod pa'i sdzas su byin gyis brlabs/ dbang po lnga la longs spyod 'gyed/ 'dod dgu s+dzas kyi char pa 'bebs/ yon tan mgron du gyur pa yi/ sa bdag klu gnyan 'khor 
8b4(tha): bcas la/ byin gyis brlabs pa'i mchod yin 'di/ bshams nas khyed la 'bul lags kyi/ mchod pa khyed kyi dmigs yul du/ ci 'dod phun sum tshogs nas kyang / bdag dang 
8b5(tha): rgyu sbyor yin bdag gis/ bder gshegs gzhal yas gnas brtsigs par/ dkar po dge ba'i las bsgrub na/ khyed kyang dge ba'i sdong gdab cing / brtan pa'i gzhi gnas stsal du 
8b6(tha): gsol/ o~ na ma stbas ti lo ka pra ti sa ma ya mu yi ha ra thim thim yaishA/ zhes dkar gyi mchod pa phyogs bzhi dbus lnga ru 'brul zhing / brtyan pa'i gzhi gnas bslang / 
9a1(tha): bar mdzad do// de nas yang ston pas bde bar gzegs pa sum gyi dkyil 'khor las/ dkyil 'khor brtsig pa'i csho ga mdhad// ren po tche's pag dang / bbra shis
9a2(tha): kyis na rnams blangs nas/ zung bzhi logs brgyad du bcad nas/ tshigs su bcad de gsungs pa/ mi 'gyur gsung du bon gyi dbyings dkyil na/ dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor ye nas 
9a3(tha): grub pa la/ gdan dang po brang bsgrub lha mi 'tshal te/ bdag dang mtha' yas sems can thams cad kyis/ sgo gsum 'du 'dzi g.yeng ba'i tshogs sangs shing / sgo gsum dge ba'i 
9a4(tha): las la 'dun spyod phyir/ bder gshegs gzhal yas po brang gnas brtsigs nas/ 'jig 'dral med par yongs su brtan gyur cig/ o~M na ma sad la a ya re ma kha bu r te 
9a5(tha): gar ma la ho/ zhes gsungs nas/ gu bzhi dpangs dang chag tshad ldan pa ru brtsigs par mdzad do// de nas yang ston pas bde bar gshegs pa yum gyi dkyil 'khor las/ chag chag 
9a6(tha): gdab cing thig gdab par mdzad de/ gtsang ma'i chab lnga dang / bdud rtsi sman yongs sbyar nas tshigs su bcad de gsungs pa/ mi 'gyur g.yung drung bon gyi dbyings dkyil na/ dbyings 
9b1(tha): kyi dkyil 'khor ye nas dag pa la/ gtsang ma'i tshan gyis chag chag mi 'tshal te/ bdag dang mtha' yas sems can thams cad kyi/ nyon mongs bag chags dri ma dag bya'i phyir/ 
9b2(tha): gtsang ma'i tshan songs chag chag 'di 'debs pas/ nyon mongs drug lnga'i dra ma dag gyur cig/ o na ma teng nam zhim pod da ras sa le sang sgeshA/ zhes tshan songs kyis chag 
9b3(tha): chag gdab par mdzad do// de nas cig gdab par mdzad de/ shzhon gtsang ma'i thig thag la/ g bur dang mtshal gyis byugs nas/ thabs shes rab dang sbyar te tshegs su bcad de 
9b4(tha): gsungs pa/ mi 'gyur g.sung dung bon gyi dbyings dkyil na/ dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor ye nas gsal ba la/ sgyu ma'i tshen gyis cig gdab mi 'tshal te/ bdag dang mtha' yas 
9b5(tha): sems can thams cad kyi/ ma rig ma mthong snang yor bsal ba'i phyir/ dkar dmar shizhin chen gyis cig gdab pas/ ma rig rmongs pa'i leng tshig gsal gyur cig/ A+o~M na ma 
9b6(tha): drang ta la mu ye ha ra khi khar sa le yais hA/ zhes cig thag brkyangs nas gdab ste/ de yang dang por mtha'i thig bzhi gdab/ de nas phyogs mtshams 'byed pa'i thig bzhi gdab/ 
10a1(tha): mtha' thigso nas bzung la lhags roe' tig bzhi gdab/ de nas dbus kyi rgya grams nas su/ zud cig mtshams su bzung la riam gsum dbye/ rim gsum bar du 
10a2(tha): skor tcheg bcu yai gdab/ skor cig nang du gdung ma'i thig bzhi bskor/ po brang gsum char bgs la sgo cig rkyang re gdab/ de nas bar skor 'byed cig snyoms pa ru/ phyi nang 'byung 
10a3(tha): rtsig 'dod yin ya gad za r tshogs/ dar bu khad las sogs pa them par gdab/ de nas nang skor pad ma'i gzhung thig brkyang / gling dang zhing khams 'byed cig gzhung la sbyar/ pho brang 
10a4(tha): / skor thig rim pa lnga ru bskor/ de ltar kun tu cha snyoms them par gdab/ ces bya ste/ dkyil 'khor gyi chag chag gdab cing / thig gdab par bstan pa'o// de nas yang ston pas / 
10a5(tha): bde bar gshegs pa yum gyi dkyil 'khor las/ dag cing gtsang ba'i tcho ga mdzad de/ thig mar bar du gcod pa'i bgegs bsal te/ rnga ghang rol mo'i sgra bsgrags nas/ gser 
10a6(tha): dang nungs dkar tsogs te tshigs su bcad de gsungs pa/ o dang gi gtsang ma'i gnas 'di ru/ stong nyid ye zhes ma rtogs shing / pha rol bhyin par mi gnas pa'i/ nyon mongs 
10b1(tha): bag la rgyu ba yi/ bgegs chen bsam pa ngan gtong ba'i/ bar du gcod pa'i gdon rnams dang / gnod par byed pa'i bgegs rnams kun/ bgegs kyi sbyor ba rgyun chod la/ rang rang /

22a4(tha2): ma ha ra tsakra ye s hA/ bso +oM na kzher ha ra tsakra yae s hA/ bs Ao~M zhi la ha ra tsakra yai s hA/ bs oM khri gsal bu ha ra bhud ha yis hA/ bs +oM smri ta ha ra byud ha ye s hA//

22a6(tha2): sahA/ bs +oM ska zhi ha r byud ha yai sw hA/ bs +o~M na ting ha ra byud dha yi s hA/ bs oM u rni ha rA b+hud ha yi sw hA/ bs o~M ha lo ha ra byud ha yai sw hA/ bso +o~M na seng ha r byund / 
22b1(tha2): ha yi s hA/ bso o~M khri mang ha ra byud ha yis hA/ bso o~M khri gsal ha ra rad na yais hA/ bso oM b+hu b+ha ha ra rad na yi s hA/ bs o~M bg+hu ya ha ra rad na yi s hA/ bs oM u / 
22b2(tha2): li ha ra rad na yaeshA/ bs oM ga rgyum ha ra rad na yis hA/ bs oM gu ci ha ra rad na yeshA/ bs oM khrosg ha ra rad na yaes hA/ bs oM lska ra ha ra rad na yes hA/ bso 
22b3(tha2): Ao~M khang ci ha ra rad na yais hA/ bs oM sna gyad ha ra rad na yais hA/ bse oM gyar dun ha ra rad na yes hA/ bs oM ra s+mi ha ra rad na ye hA/ bs oM gu smri mar la ha ra rad / 
22b4(tha2): na yes hA/ bso o khri gsal ha ra kzher zhi yeshA/ bso oM dung mu ha ra kher zhi yeshA/ bs oM kher lo ha ra kher zhi yas hA/ bs oM gu yo ha ra zher ni yes hA/ bso / 
22b5(tha2): AoM khri ma ha ra kher zhi yae s hA/ bse oM a dkar ha ra kher zhi ye s hA/ bso A+o~M lo ka ha ra zher zhi yae s hA/ bs oM bhud +ha ha ra kher zhi yai s hA/ bs +oM tsakra ha ra zher / 
22b6(tha2): zhi yeshA/ bso o~M par+ha ha ra kher zhi yes hA/ bs oM ka rma ha ra kher zhi yes hA/ bs oM rad+ha ha ra kher zhi yes hA/ bs oM a ma ha ra kher zhi yes hA/ bso +o~M a /

24a1(tha2): stha/ bs o~ na ma de rgya ya sangs ma rgyu y/ phyi ma yi sang tshangs la sungs ni de rgya yashA/ bs o~ na ma dung mu de rgya sangs ma rgyu s/ phyi ma yi sangs tshangs /
